 \"text\": \"The Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) implementation spans two main areas:\\n\\n**1. Service & Policy Evaluation (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleService** (`IndexLifecycleService.java`): The central service that triggers policy evaluation. It listens to cluster state changes, checks if ILM is enabled, and invokes the `IndexLifecycleRunner` to run policy steps for each managed index. It is triggered both on master election (for async action steps) and on cluster state updates (for cluster state action/wait steps).\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleRunner** (`IndexLifecycleRunner.java`): Orchestrates the execution of individual lifecycle steps. It dispatches to the appropriate execution path depending on step type: `ClusterStateActionStep`, `ClusterStateWaitStep`, `AsyncActionStep`, or `AsyncWaitStep`.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleTransition** (`IndexLifecycleTransition.java`): Handles transitions between steps and phases in the lifecycle state machine.\\n\\n- **ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (`ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java`): A cluster state update task that runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps synchronously within a cluster state update.\\n\\n- **MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java`): Updates the cluster state to advance an index to the next step.\\n\\n- **MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask.java`): Moves an index into the ILM error step when a step fails.\\n\\n- **SetStepInfoUpdateTask** (`SetStepInfoUpdateTask.java`): Updates step info in index metadata.\\n\\n- **PolicyStepsRegistry** (`PolicyStepsRegistry.java`): Maintains a registry of compiled step lists for each policy, keyed by policy name and version.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycle** (`IndexLifecycle.java`): The X-Pack plugin class registering ILM components.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask** (`IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask.java`): Base class for ILM cluster state update tasks.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleFeatures** (`IndexLifecycleFeatures.java`): Defines ILM feature metadata for the features API.\\n\\n- **IlmHealthIndicatorService** (`IlmHealthIndicatorService.java`): Health API integration for ILM.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider** (`ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider.java`): Handles reserved state (file-based) ILM policy management.\\n\\n**2. Transport Action Handlers (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/)**\\n\\n- **TransportPutLifecycleAction** (`TransportPutLifecycleAction.java`): Handles PUT policy requests, storing `LifecyclePolicy` objects into cluster state via `IndexLifecycleMetadata`.\\n\\n- **TransportDeleteLifecycleAction** (`TransportDeleteLifecycleAction.java`): Handles DELETE policy requests.\\n\\n- **TransportGetLifecycleAction**, **TransportExplainLifecycleAction**, **TransportGetStatusAction**, **TransportMigrateToDataTiersAction**, **TransportMoveToStepAction**, **TransportRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction**, **TransportRetryAction**, **TransportStartILMAction**, **TransportStopILMAction**: Additional transport action handlers for various ILM operations.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleAction** (`ReservedLifecycleAction.java`): Reserved cluster state handler that applies ILM policies from configuration files.\\n\\n- REST handlers: `RestPutLifecycleAction`, `RestDeleteLifecycleAction`, `RestGetLifecycleAction`, `RestExplainLifecycleAction`, `RestGetStatusAction`, `RestMigrateToDataTiersAction`, `RestMoveToStepAction`, `RestRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction`, `RestRetryAction`, `RestStartILMAction`, `RestStopAction`.\\n\\n**3. ILM History (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/history/)**\\n\\n- **ILMHistoryStore**, **ILMHistoryItem**, **ILMHistoryTemplateRegistry**: Record ILM step execution history to the `.ilm-history-*` index.\\n\\n**4. Cluster Metadata Helper (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService** (`MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService.java`): Logic for migrating index/data stream allocation to data tiers.\\n\\n**5. Model Classes & Step Framework (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **LifecyclePolicy** (`LifecyclePolicy.java`): Top-level model class representing a named ILM policy composed of named `Phase` objects.\\n\\n- **Phase** (`Phase.java`): Represents a lifecycle phase (hot, warm, cold, frozen, delete) with a minimum age and a set of `LifecycleAction` objects.\\n\\n- **Step** (`Step.java`): Base class for all lifecycle steps with a `StepKey` (phase/action/name triple).\\n\\n- **ClusterStateActionStep** (`ClusterStateActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform synchronous cluster state modifications (e.g., `InitializePolicyContextStep`, `GenerateUniqueIndexNameStep`, `CopySettingsStep`).\\n\\n- **ClusterStateWaitStep** (`ClusterStateWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that check a condition synchronously against cluster state.\\n\\n- **AsyncActionStep** (`AsyncActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform asynchronous actions against the cluster (e.g., `ShrinkStep`, `RolloverStep`, `ForceMergeStep`, `DownsampleStep`).\\n\\n- **AsyncWaitStep** (`AsyncWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that asynchronously poll a condition (e.g., `WaitForRolloverReadyStep`, `WaitForSnapshotStep`, `SegmentCountStep`).\\n\\n**6. LifecycleExecutionState (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **LifecycleExecutionState** (`LifecycleExecutionState.java`): Stored in index metadata (custom metadata map), tracks the current lifecycle step (phase, action, step names), step start times, phase definition cache, and failure information for each ILM-managed index.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6000,"cache_read_input_tokens":42086,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":6000,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":10,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"867e14a9-fd60-47d2-9fc1-01805ad7b9d4","uuid":"668dd28d-e5b6-441b-a9bf-310231ce56ed"}

 \"text\": \"The Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) implementation spans several modules:\\n\\n**1. Core Service & Policy Evaluation (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleService** (`IndexLifecycleService.java`): The central service that triggers policy evaluation. It listens to cluster state changes and master elections, then invokes `IndexLifecycleRunner` to run policy steps for each managed index. On master election it runs `AsyncActionStep` steps; on cluster state changes it runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps, and schedules periodic polling for `AsyncWaitStep` steps.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleRunner** (`IndexLifecycleRunner.java`): Orchestrates execution of individual lifecycle steps, dispatching to the correct execution path based on step type.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleTransition** (`IndexLifecycleTransition.java`): Manages transitions between steps and phases.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycle** (`IndexLifecycle.java`): The X-Pack plugin registration class for all ILM components.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask** (`IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask.java`): Base class for cluster state update tasks used by ILM.\\n\\n- **ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (`ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java`): Cluster state update task that runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps synchronously.\\n\\n- **MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java`): Updates cluster state to advance an index to the next step.\\n\\n- **MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask.java`): Moves an index into the ILM error step on failure.\\n\\n- **SetStepInfoUpdateTask** (`SetStepInfoUpdateTask.java`): Updates step info stored in index metadata.\\n\\n- **PolicyStepsRegistry** (`PolicyStepsRegistry.java`): Maintains a compiled cache of step lists per policy.\\n\\n- **IlmHealthIndicatorService** (`IlmHealthIndicatorService.java`): Health API integration for ILM status.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider** (`ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider.java`): Handles file-based reserved cluster state ILM policies.\\n\\n**2. Transport & REST Action Handlers (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/)**\\n\\n- **TransportPutLifecycleAction**: Handles PUT policy requests, storing `LifecyclePolicy` into cluster state via `IndexLifecycleMetadata`.\\n- **TransportDeleteLifecycleAction**: Handles DELETE policy requests.\\n- **TransportGetLifecycleAction**, **TransportExplainLifecycleAction**, **TransportGetStatusAction**, **TransportMigrateToDataTiersAction**, **TransportMoveToStepAction**, **TransportRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction**, **TransportRetryAction**, **TransportStartILMAction**, **TransportStopILMAction**: Additional transport handlers for ILM operations.\\n- **ReservedLifecycleAction**: Reserved state handler that uses `TransportPutLifecycleAction` and `TransportDeleteLifecycleAction` internally.\\n- REST handlers: `RestPutLifecycleAction`, `RestDeleteLifecycleAction`, `RestGetLifecycleAction`, `RestExplainLifecycleAction`, `RestGetStatusAction`, `RestMigrateToDataTiersAction`, `RestMoveToStepAction`, `RestRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction`, `RestRetryAction`, `RestStartILMAction`, `RestStopAction`.\\n\\n**3. ILM History (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/history/)**\\n\\n- **ILMHistoryStore**, **ILMHistoryItem**, **ILMHistoryTemplateRegistry**: Record ILM step execution history to the `.ilm-history-*` index.\\n\\n**4. Cluster Metadata Helper (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService**: Logic for migrating index/data stream allocation to data tiers.\\n\\n**5. Model Classes & Step Framework (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **LifecyclePolicy** (`LifecyclePolicy.java`): Top-level model representing a named ILM policy composed of named `Phase` objects.\\n- **Phase** (`Phase.java`): Represents a lifecycle phase (hot, warm, cold, frozen, delete) with a minimum age and a set of `LifecycleAction` objects.\\n- **Step** (`Step.java`): Base class for all lifecycle steps, identified by a `StepKey` (phase/action/name triple).\\n- **ClusterStateActionStep** (`ClusterStateActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform synchronous cluster state modifications.\\n- **ClusterStateWaitStep** (`ClusterStateWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that check a condition synchronously against cluster state.\\n- **AsyncActionStep** (`AsyncActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps performing asynchronous transport actions (e.g., `ShrinkStep`, `RolloverStep`, `ForceMergeStep`).\\n- **AsyncWaitStep** (`AsyncWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that periodically poll a condition asynchronously (e.g., `WaitForRolloverReadyStep`, `WaitForSnapshotStep`, `SegmentCountStep`).\\n\\n**6. LifecycleExecutionState (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **LifecycleExecutionState** (`LifecycleExecutionState.java`): Stored in each index's custom metadata, tracking the current lifecycle step (phase, action, step names), step start times, phase definition cache, and failure details for each ILM-managed index.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":355,"cache_read_input_tokens":57602,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":355,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"867e14a9-fd60-47d2-9fc1-01805ad7b9d4","uuid":"e329f33e-f0a6-4c3f-b22e-e5079dbc05b8"}

 \"text\": \"The Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) implementation spans several modules:\\n\\n**1. Core Service & Policy Evaluation (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleService** (`IndexLifecycleService.java`): The central service that triggers policy evaluation. It listens to cluster state changes and master elections, then invokes `IndexLifecycleRunner` to run policy steps for each managed index. On master election it runs `AsyncActionStep` steps; on cluster state changes it runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps, and schedules periodic polling for `AsyncWaitStep` steps.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleRunner** (`IndexLifecycleRunner.java`): Orchestrates execution of individual lifecycle steps, dispatching to the correct execution path based on step type.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleTransition** (`IndexLifecycleTransition.java`): Manages transitions between steps and phases.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycle** (`IndexLifecycle.java`): The X-Pack plugin registration class for all ILM components.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask** (`IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask.java`): Base class for cluster state update tasks used by ILM.\\n\\n- **ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (`ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java`): Cluster state update task that runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps synchronously.\\n\\n- **MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java`): Updates cluster state to advance an index to the next step.\\n\\n- **MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask.java`): Moves an index into the ILM error step on failure.\\n\\n- **SetStepInfoUpdateTask** (`SetStepInfoUpdateTask.java`): Updates step info stored in index metadata.\\n\\n- **PolicyStepsRegistry** (`PolicyStepsRegistry.java`): Maintains a compiled cache of step lists per policy.\\n\\n- **IlmHealthIndicatorService** (`IlmHealthIndicatorService.java`): Health API integration for ILM status.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider** (`ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider.java`): Handles file-based reserved cluster state ILM policies.\\n\\n**2. Transport & REST Action Handlers (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/)**\\n\\n- **TransportPutLifecycleAction**: Handles PUT policy requests, storing `LifecyclePolicy` into cluster state via `IndexLifecycleMetadata`.\\n- **TransportDeleteLifecycleAction**: Handles DELETE policy requests.\\n- **TransportGetLifecycleAction**, **TransportExplainLifecycleAction**, **TransportGetStatusAction**, **TransportMigrateToDataTiersAction**, **TransportMoveToStepAction**, **TransportRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction**, **TransportRetryAction**, **TransportStartILMAction**, **TransportStopILMAction**: Additional transport handlers for ILM operations.\\n- **ReservedLifecycleAction**: Reserved state handler that uses `TransportPutLifecycleAction` and `TransportDeleteLifecycleAction` internally.\\n- REST handlers: `RestPutLifecycleAction`, `RestDeleteLifecycleAction`, `RestGetLifecycleAction`, `RestExplainLifecycleAction`, `RestGetStatusAction`, `RestMigrateToDataTiersAction`, `RestMoveToStepAction`, `RestRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction`, `RestRetryAction`, `RestStartILMAction`, `RestStopAction`.\\n\\n**3. ILM History (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/history/)**\\n\\n- **ILMHistoryStore**, **ILMHistoryItem**, **ILMHistoryTemplateRegistry**: Record ILM step execution history to the `.ilm-history-*` index.\\n\\n**4. Cluster Metadata Helper (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService**: Logic for migrating index/data stream allocation to data tiers.\\n\\n**5. Model Classes & Step Framework (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **LifecyclePolicy** (`LifecyclePolicy.java`): Top-level model representing a named ILM policy composed of named `Phase` objects.\\n- **Phase** (`Phase.java`): Represents a lifecycle phase (hot, warm, cold, frozen, delete) with a minimum age and a set of `LifecycleAction` objects.\\n- **Step** (`Step.java`): Base class for all lifecycle steps, identified by a `StepKey` (phase/action/name triple).\\n- **ClusterStateActionStep** (`ClusterStateActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform synchronous cluster state modifications.\\n- **ClusterStateWaitStep** (`ClusterStateWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that check a condition synchronously against cluster state.\\n- **AsyncActionStep** (`AsyncActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps performing asynchronous transport actions (e.g., `ShrinkStep`, `RolloverStep`, `ForceMergeStep`).\\n- **AsyncWaitStep** (`AsyncWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that periodically poll a condition asynchronously (e.g., `WaitForRolloverReadyStep`, `WaitForSnapshotStep`, `SegmentCountStep`).\\n\\n**6. LifecycleExecutionState (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **LifecycleExecutionState** (`LifecycleExecutionState.java`): Stored in each index's custom metadata, tracking the current lifecycle step (phase, action, step names), step start times, phase definition cache, and failure details for each ILM-managed index.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
